function keyboardClick(element) {

  ele.outerFind(element).keydown(function(e) {

    if (e.keyCode === 13 || e.keyCode === 32) {

      e.preventDefault();

      this.click();

    }

  });

}



function ariaExpand(btn) {

  btn.attr('aria-expanded', 'false');

  btn.click(function() {

    if ($ae(this).attr('aria-expanded') === "false") {

      $ae(this).attr('aria-expanded', 'true');

    } else {

      $ae(this).attr('aria-expanded', 'false');

    }

  });

}

ele.outerFind('form.vv-lookup-form, form.vv-estimate-form').submit(function() {

  var errormsgs = $ae(this).find('.field p.error');

  errormsgs.each(function() {

    if (!$ae(this).attr('id')) {

      $ae(this).attr('id', 'ae_id' + Math.floor(Math.random() * 1000));

    }

  });

  $ae(this).find('input, select').each(function() {

    $ae(this).attr('aria-describedby', $ae(this).next('.error').attr('id'));

  });



  AudioEye.focusElement(errormsgs.eq(0).prev('input, select'));

});

// AEI-139020 Filter cars tabset

ele.outerFind('cars-filters .srp-filters').each(function() {

  var tabs = $ae(this).find('.filter-tabs .tab');

  var tablist = $ae(this).find('.filter-tabs');



  tabs.attr('role', 'tab');

  tablist.attr('role', 'tablist');

  tablist.find('div[cars-shop-srp-filters]').attr('role', 'tabpanel');



  // using tabs.eq(0) as selected because there are no other selectors to use for selected & refreshing the page changes selected back to first

  tabs.eq(0).attr({'aria-selected': 'true', 'tabindex': '0'});

  tabs.not(':eq(0)').attr({'aria-selected': 'false', 'tabindex': '-1'});

  keyboardClick(tabs);





  tabs.click(function() {

    $ae(this).closest('.filter-tabs').find('.tab').not($ae(this)).attr({'aria-selected': 'false', 'tabindex': '-1'});

    $ae(this).attr({'aria-selected': 'true', 'tabindex': '0'});



    var aethis = $ae(this);

    setTimeout(function() {

      AudioEye.focusElement(aethis);

    }, 200);

  });

  AudioEye.arrowKeyLoop(ele, tabs, tablist);

});



api.hideFromAT('.srp-filters .filter-tabs input[type="radio"]');

function kbClickBtn(btn) {

  api.convertToBtn(btn);

  keyboardClick(btn);

}



function ariaExpand(btn) {

  btn.attr('aria-expanded', 'false');

  btn.click(function() {

    if ($ae(this).attr('aria-expanded') === "false") {

      $ae(this).attr('aria-expanded', 'true');

    } else {

      $ae(this).attr('aria-expanded', 'false');

    }

  });

}

ele.outerFind('.button-bar-container .button-bar li label').each(function() {

  $ae(this).attr('role', 'radio');

  if ($ae(this).closest('li').hasClass('active')) {

    $ae(this).attr({'aria-checked': 'true', 'tabindex': '0'});

  } else {

    $ae(this).attr({'aria-checked': 'false', 'tabindex': '-1'});

  }



  AudioEye.arrowKeyLoop(ele, $ae(this).closest('.button-bar').find('label'), $ae(this).closest('.button-bar'));



  keyboardClick($ae(this));

  $ae(this).click(function() {

    $ae(this).attr({'aria-checked': 'true', 'tabindex': '0'});

    $ae(this).closest('.button-bar').find('li label').not($ae(this)).attr({'aria-checked': 'false', 'tabindex': '-1'});

  });

});

// AEI-139019

$ae('.srp-filters .filters .refinements').has('.radio').each(function() {

  var radiobtns = $ae(this).find('label')

  radiobtns.attr('role', 'radio');



  radiobtns.each(function() {

    if ($ae(this).prev('input').attr('checked')) {

      $ae(this).attr({'aria-checked': 'true', 'tabindex': '0'});

    }

  });



  if (!$ae(this).find('input[checked]').length) {

    $ae(this).find('label').eq(0).attr({'aria-checked': 'true', 'tabindex': '0'});

  }

  radiobtns.not('[aria-checked]').attr({'aria-checked': 'false', 'tabindex': '-1'});



  AudioEye.arrowKeyLoop(ele, radiobtns, $ae(this));



  keyboardClick(radiobtns);

  radiobtns.click(function() {

    $ae(this).attr({'aria-checked': 'true', 'tabindex': '0'});

    $ae(this).closest('.refinements').find('label').not($ae(this)).attr({'aria-checked': 'false', 'tabindex': '-1'});

  });

});

    <script type="text/javascript">



                    var f = function (ele, api) {

                      function keyboardClick(element) {

  ele.outerFind(element).keydown(function(e) {

    if (e.keyCode === 13 || e.keyCode === 32) {

      e.preventDefault();

      this.click();

    }

  });

}





function modalFocus(trigger, closeBtn, modal) {

  ele.outerFind(trigger).each(function() {

    var clickedTrigger = $ae(this);

    $ae(this).click(function() {

      setTimeout(function() {

        AudioEye.focusElement(closeBtn);

        AudioEye.modals.enableTabLoop(modal);



        keyboardClick(closeBtn);

        api.convertToBtn(closeBtn).attr('aria-label', 'Close');



        ele.outerFind(closeBtn).click(function() {

          setTimeout(function() {

            AudioEye.focusElement(clickedTrigger);

          }, 500);

        });

      }, 1500); 

    });

  });

}

//IM-12901 AT: Home Page: Interactive elements not keyboard accessible.

ele.outerFind(".sds-tabs__list > li > a").attr({"tabindex":"-1"}).on('click keydown', function (e) {

  if(e.type === 'click'){

    setTimeout(function(){

      $ae('.sds-tabs__list > li > a[aria-selected="true"]').attr({"tabindex":"0"});

      $ae('.sds-tabs__list > li > a[aria-selected="false"]').attr({"tabindex":"-1"});

    }, 500);

  }

  if (e.keyCode === 13 || e.keyCode === 32) {

    e.preventDefault();

    $ae(this)[0].click();

  }

  

  if(e.keyCode === 37 || e.keyCode === 38){

    e.preventDefault();

    if($ae(this).parent().prev()[0]){

      AudioEye.focusElement($ae(this).parent().prev().find('a'));

    }

    else{

      AudioEye.focusElement($ae(this).closest('ul').find('a').last());

    }



  }

  if(e.keyCode === 39 || e.keyCode === 40){

    e.preventDefault();

    if($ae(this).parent().next()[0]){

      AudioEye.focusElement($ae(this).parent().next().find('a'));

    }

    else {

      AudioEye.focusElement($ae(this).closest('ul').find('a').first());

    }

  }

});
